The reauthorization will be the third reauthorization of education funding since 2000 and the first time children will have a child support payment from their education program after school and college graduation. This bill has made significant and positive contributions to students' academic achievement.  The reauthorization bill also holds up important priorities for States, such as the central requirement in Section 504 for 3 months before the school year begins, school construction funds, and the School-to-Work Partnership Program. The legislation reduces the downpayment for students on Head Start from $35,000 to $26,000. It makes the National Service Program pilot program permanent and increases student assistance to help States and the Federal Government build rural schools.

Mr. President, I rise today to pay tribute to New Hampshire Boy Scouts of America National Council members as they celebrate 100 years of serving in the State of New Hampshire.  The national council was established in 1974 by the National Boy Scouts of America [BSA] to award the highest rank available to the youngest organization in Scouting. The council is comprised of 90 adult members who choose candidates to serve on the council for their professional competence and ability to work together to help improve the lives of young people.  The council is comprised of all national grades--B, C, D, F, and with up to 70 individual Scouts, three coaches and mentors for the youth of the organization. A Member of the council serves at the discretion of a vice president, who serves as a national scout leader, president, and four advisory council members.
